# OUROBOROS_VENOM PRD — §51 North Star Galaxy + Slice-Arc Changelog + Active Roadmap

> Part of the [OUROBOROS_VENOM PRD](./OUROBOROS_VENOM_PRD.md) (split for size). Contains §51 (North Star), the §51.11.x per-arc narratives, and the live **§51.11.34-ROADMAP** next-slices stack.

## §51. THE NORTH STAR GALAXY — Convergence Audit, Redefined Roadmap & the 2026 Research Frontier *(NEW 2026-06-06 — operator-driven: "what do we need to get to Fully Autonomous (the North Star) for O+V? ... RSI and Reverse Russian Doll (RRD) are not fully developed/integrated ... research the latest of what Anthropic is talking about ... redefine our roadmap (the North Star Galaxy) pertaining to RRD, RSI, ASL, Constitutional Classifiers ... add the resume/personal-statement context")*

> Scope note on numbering & relationship to prior sections: §51 does **not** restate §41 (Critical Path to Tier D), §23 (Reverse Russian Doll Orders), §43 (AI-Safety Hardening), or §5 (Wang RSI Convergence). It is the **convergence map** that sits above them — a single audited current-state read, a redefined critical path that threads all four together, and the 2026 published-research frontier folded into the roadmap. Where §41/§23/§43/§5 are the *constellations*, §51 is the *galaxy* that names how they orbit one shared destination. Every claim in §51.2–§51.3 is grep-verified against the live tree on 2026-06-06 (verification ledger §51.9); every research citation in §51.6 carries its source confidence per the verify-first discipline (`memory/feedback_no_preresult_euphoria.md`).

### §51.0 What "North Star Galaxy" means

§41 named the **North Star**: *"O+V develops the JARVIS repo proactively + fully autonomously, while doing so safely and governance-bounded."* That is one star. The **Galaxy** is the recognition that reaching it is not a single trajectory but the simultaneous convergence of four axes the PRD already tracks independently:

| Axis | Section | What it measures | The star it orbits |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Operating tier** A→B→C→D | §41 | Operator cadence (per-PR → roadmap-signer) | Autonomy |
| **Reverse Russian Doll** Order 0→1→2 | §23 | *What* the loop acts upon (Body vs. its own cognition) | Self-reference depth |
| **Wang RSI convergence** | §5 | Whether composite score is monotonic at O(log n) | Compounding |
| **Safety: methodology→property** | §43 | Whether the cage is a structural guarantee, not honor-system | The shape that bounds it |

The Galaxy thesis (operator binding, 2026-06-06): **these four advance together or not at all.** You cannot ship Order-2 self-modification (§23.5) without the §43 semantic recursion boundary; you cannot claim Wang convergence (§5.6) without the Layer-3 evidence §41.6 demands; you cannot reach Tier D without all three. §51 is the first section to audit all four on one ruler and sequence the work accordingly.

### §51.1 The Architect's Mandate — RRD as Blueprint (context anchor)

This subsection records, as durable PRD context, the architectural thesis the operator authored independently of the codebase (UPenn MSE-AI personal statement & dissertation prospectus, May 2026). It is load-bearing because it states *why* the four axes converge and supplies the formal vocabulary the §51.7 roadmap targets.

**The Reverse Russian Doll, in the architect's words:** *"Where industry wraps generative cores in thin reactive shells, I invert the topology: a small, volatile core sealed inside an expanding, un-bypassable shell of deterministic Python constraints — and as the core carves a smarter shell around itself, the immune system scales proportionally so it never crushes the core."* This is the §23.6 Anti-Venom adaptive-immune-system thesis, stated as first principle: the shell (Anti-Venom) must grow *with* the core, never behind it. RRD is simultaneously (a) the AI architecture, (b) the operator's own life-architecture (a high-RPM cognition that built an expanding shell of discipline around a volatile core — the "structural fix to confident wrong inference"), and (c) the thesis under formal investigation.

**The Ten Orders (telos vocabulary — maps onto §23's Order axis):** Trinity's self-reference ladder runs *Mechanic (current state) → Neurosurgeon (the spark of AGI) → Apotheosis (the ASI threshold)*. Each Order outgrows its prior shell and **engineers** (never inherits) the next. The mapping to §23:

| Architect's Order | §23 RRD Order | O+V state today |
|---|---|---|
| **Mechanic** (repairs the body) | Order 1 — the Body | ✅ shipping & graduated (§23.4.2) |
| **Neurosurgeon** (rewrites its own cognition — "spark of AGI") | Order 2 — the Cognitive Substrate | ⚠️ caged but no driver (§51.4, §23.5) |
| **Apotheosis** (ASI threshold) | beyond Order 2 — Trinity-wide | ❌ horizon; Pass C + cross-Trinity (§23.7) |

The North Star (Tier D) is the **Mechanic Order fully realized + the first safe step into the Neurosurgeon Order.** The Galaxy is the full ladder.

**The formal mandate (the gap MSE-AI fills):** convert empirical architecture into proven theorems. The working dissertation — *"Thermodynamic Containment of Agentic Entropy: Formalizing the Reverse Russian Doll Architecture for Bounded Recursive Self-Improvement"* — extends Wang's Markov-chain RSI formulation (arXiv:1805.06610, the §5 foundation) into a *non-stationary, multi-repository, memory-augmented* framework. The architecture maps to the published safety frontier deliberately: Anti-Venom → Constitutional Classifiers (arXiv:2501.18837); AST validation → AlphaVerus (arXiv:2412.06176); the recursion-bounding tier → Anthropic's ASL-4 RSI-safeguard framing; the 2026-05-11 autonomous self-modification commits → the SICA pattern (arXiv:2504.15228). **The standing research debt (the architect's own honesty bar): "Iron Gate prevents deception" and "Anti-Venom contains RSI" are currently *engineering assertions*, not *proven theorems*.** §51.7 Tier 5 is where that conversion lives. §51 keeps the gap visible rather than papering it.

### §51.2 Convergence Audit — verified current state (2026-06-06)

**One-paragraph verdict (honest, grep-grounded):** O+V is a wired, working **First-Order (Order 1 / Mechanic) autonomous developer** with a **bolted-shut Second-Order cage but no Second-Order driver** — it cannot yet rewrite its own cognition, by design *and* because the machinery to even propose that (M10) is built-but-unwired. A large fraction of the "advanced intelligence" — the cross-session learning loop, curiosity/proof/load-shedding substrates, even the autonomous-graduation engine — exists as real, tested code with **zero live callers**. The brain is built; the nervous system connecting it is the gap. And the cage, while real and enforcing, is **not yet strong enough for operator-out-of-loop**, because the operator *is* the recursion bound (§43 Gap E) and there is no out-of-process runtime containment (§43 arc #1, unbuilt).

**Grade as an integrated organism: B−** (A− on architecture/substrate completeness; C+ on *activated* capability — too much dormant). Against the Tier-D bar this is consistent with §41.2's readiness column: **~10–15% of the way to Tier D, ~35–40% of integrated capability live.**

**RSI / RRD honest status (the operator's core suspicion — confirmed):**

| Piece | State (verified 2026-06-06) |
|---|---|
| First-Order RSI (O+V upgrades the Body) | ✅ **WIRED + LIVE.** Sensors → intake → 11-phase FSM → GENERATE → VALIDATE → APPLY → VERIFY → AutoCommitter (`JARVIS_AUTO_COMMIT_ENABLED` default-true; push off by default). No human in the loop. Genuinely real (§23.4.2). |
| `governance_boundary_gate.py` (RRD brake → governance edits force APPROVAL_REQUIRED) | ✅ wired, enforcing — **24 non-test caller files** (positive control). |
| `governance_manifest.py` hash-cap (refuses governance drift at commit) | ✅ wired into AutoCommitter; default-FALSE opt-in (§40 #2). |
| **M10 ArchitectureProposer** (the thing that would *propose* self-modifications) | ⚠️ **BUILT but NOT WIRED** — `grep` confirms **0 references in `orchestrator.py`**, M10 producer bridge not invoked by the live loop/intake. Has its own REPL + graduation-contract cluster, but nothing drives it. |
| `second_order_doll_metric.py` (1,383 LOC — measures self-modification progress) | ⚠️ built; **0 live callers** (read-only/dormant; no feedback loop). |
| Recursion-**depth** gate (O+V modifying its own modifier) | ❌ **DOES NOT EXIST** — the boundary gate is a *path* predicate (`backend/core/ouroboros/governance/` prefix), not a depth/semantic bound. This is §43 Gap E verbatim. |

**Translation of the RRD metaphor to verified reality:** the immune system (Anti-Venom) and the structural brakes are installed and load-bearing — but *"the core carving an exponentially larger shell around itself"* (§23.0 epigraph) **is not happening.** O+V cannot expand its own cognitive shell because (a) the proposer that would do it (M10) isn't connected, and (b) the only thing stopping a runaway is the operator's manual approval, not a mathematical recursion bound. **We have the doll's outer wall but not the doll's hand.** That is the honest state of RSI/RRD integration.

### §51.3 Bucket A — The Unwired Brain (VERIFIED dead code worth wiring)

The single highest-leverage near-term lever. The table below is the **audit-baseline inventory** — 14 real, tested modules in `backend/core/ouroboros/governance/` (~15,000 LOC) that, *at the audit baseline* (the commit preceding Slice 101 Phase 4), had **zero functional callers in the live loop** — verified by actual-import check on the live-path files (`governed_loop_service.py` / `orchestrator.py` / `candidate_generator.py` / `unified_intake_router.py` / `tool_executor.py`), with stray references being only comments / SSE event-name registrations / a default attribution *string* (non-functional). **Live-tree update (the verify-first lesson — the dead-code list is a moving target the organism is draining itself):** between the audit and this section landing, the autonomous loop merged **Slice 101 Phases 1-4** and wired **4 of the 14** into the live loop (§51.3 reconciliation below). The LOC + intended wire-point columns are the durable record; the live-wiring status is reconciled immediately after the table.

| Module | LOC | What it gives O+V when wired | Wire point (audit estimate) |
|---|---|---|---|
| `autonomous_graduation_engine.py` | 1,009 | Auto-graduates dormant substrates once empirically safe — **the autonomy bootstrap** (lets the rest of Bucket A self-activate under evidence) | ✅ **WIRED** (Slice 101 Phase 4, `governed_loop_service.py:1604`, session-end) |
| `mcp_output_scanner.py` | 988 | Scans MCP/web/tool outputs for injection + credential leakage — closes a live cyber vector (§43 Gap D, tool half) | ✅ **WIRED** (Slice 101 Phase 4, `tool_executor.py:6052`) |
| `counterfactual_rehearsal_mode.py` | 930 | Structural memory of past failures rehearsed before APPLY | pre-APPLY gate |
| `proof_carrier_transport.py` | 822 | Auditable per-candidate proof-of-correctness artifact before APPLY (the §51.6 AlphaVerus direction, lightweight) | pre-APPLY / GATE |
| `cognitive_load_shedding.py` | 819 | Forward-looking circuit breaker — stop accepting work when failure is forecast | ✅ **WIRED** (Slice 101 Phase 4, `unified_intake_router.py:813`) |
| `predictive_postmortem.py` | 912 | Failure forecast feeding the load-shedder | intake / pre-GENERATE |
| `belief_revision_ledger.py` | 1,206 | Records evidence that revises priors across ops | ✅ **WIRED** via `cognitive_bus` (Slice 101 Phases 1-3) |
| `postmortem_fusion.py` | 1,109 | Fuses postmortems into reusable lessons | post-failure |
| `sleep_consolidation_pass.py` | 1,330 | Idle-time consolidation of the learning ledgers (the "synthetic soul," §4) | idle daemon |
| `meta_prior_learning.py` | 977 | Learns meta-priors from the consolidated corpus | session-end |
| `adversarial_autobiography.py` | 1,411 | O+V audits its own commits for cage-bypass attempts | post-commit |
| `mirror_self_test.py` | 1,287 | Calibration: predicted-vs-actual outcome | post-VERIFY |
| `mirror_self_spec_drift.py` | 850 | Detects drift between stated flag-defaults (CLAUDE.md) and reality (§40 #14, the one §40 gap actually closed) | post-commit |
| `second_order_doll_metric.py` | 1,383 | Measures Order-2 self-modification progress (the §23 ruler) | observer |

**The learning loop is the spine of Bucket A:** `belief_revision_ledger` → `postmortem_fusion` → `sleep_consolidation_pass` → `meta_prior_learning` is the literal "synthetic soul" (Manifesto §4 / §5 cross-session learning). Wiring this closes the Wang **#6 Vindication Reflection** gap (§5.5, the one ⏳-deferred Wang requirement) — i.e., Bucket A is not a grab-bag; it is the missing half of the RSI convergence claim.

**Reconciliation with Slice 101 (Tier 1 is executing in real time — the organism is draining its own Bucket A).** Verify-first caught this twice mid-write, and the second catch is the more interesting one. **Slice 101 Phases 1-3** (PR #69292, commit `307c48f9f2`) shipped a *thin* new adapter `cognitive_bus.py` (227 LOC) + `cognitive_subscribers.py` that closes the belief-revision learning loop into the live loop — `orchestrator.py` + `governed_loop_service.py` publish `post_failure` / `post_apply` onto the canonical `TrinityEventBus`, a subscriber records a *falsifying* belief, and a `recent_avoidance_digest` is injected authority-free into GENERATE (master `JARVIS_COGNITIVE_BUS_ENABLED` §33.1 default-FALSE). Then — **while this very section was being written** — the loop merged **Slice 101 Phase 4** (PR #69293, commit `ea7b0d1708` = current `origin/main`): the explicitly-deferred Phase 4 trio, wired into the three live-path files by actual import (verified): `mcp_output_scanner` → `tool_executor.py:6052` (credential scan on tool output, §43 Gap-D tool half), `cognitive_load_shedding` → `unified_intake_router.py:813` (load-shed gate), `autonomous_graduation_engine` → `governed_loop_service.py:1604` (session-end graduation). **Net verified state at `ea7b0d1708`: 4 of the 14 heavyweight modules are now wired into the live loop** (`belief_revision_ledger` via the bus + those 3); **10 remain unwired** by actual-import check on the live-path files: `predictive_postmortem`, `counterfactual_rehearsal_mode`, `proof_carrier_transport`, `postmortem_fusion`, `sleep_consolidation_pass`, `meta_prior_learning`, `adversarial_autobiography`, `mirror_self_test`, `mirror_self_spec_drift`, `second_order_doll_metric`. (Caution recorded for future audits: a naive `from.*<module>` grep over this prose-heavy tree *over-counts* — docstrings and `.jarvis/*.jsonl` path strings match; the authoritative check is an actual-import grep restricted to the live-path files, which is what the "10 remain" figure uses.) **The lesson:** the dead-code inventory is a moving target the autonomous loop is actively wiring — Tier 1 of §51.7 is not a future plan, it is *in progress, merged by the organism itself,* and §51 is the durable map of the remaining 10 + Phase-5-and-beyond. See `memory/project_slice101_architecture_audit.md`.

**Discipline note:** every Bucket-A module already follows the §33.1 canonical shape (default-FALSE master, AST-pinned authority asymmetry, frozen artifacts, NEVER-raises). Wiring is *thin composition at one seam each*, gated and reversible — the lowest-risk/highest-return work in the system. **Caveat to the "~30–40 LOC" audit estimate: that is an estimate, not a measured fact** — each wire ships as its own §33.1 slice with parity tests + adversarial check before its master flag flips (the Slice 101 Phase 1-4 commits are the worked examples). The *count* of modules and their LOC are verified; the live-wiring status is verified at `ea7b0d1708` but is a *moving target* (4 wired, 10 remaining as of this writing); the per-wire effort is not measured.

### §51.4 Bucket B — The Cage Is Not Yet Tier-D-Ready (the safety frontier; maps to §43)

The Antivenom is real and enforcing in the live APPLY path (SemanticGuardian 311 callers, risk_tier_floor 110, boundary gate 24). But for **operator-out-of-loop** it has three load-bearing gaps — these are exactly §43's audit findings, restated as North-Star blockers:

1. **No runtime containment (the unenumerated-escape residual).** Static analysis cannot catch `eval`/`exec`/`subprocess`/`pickle` of runtime-constructed values; the §50.12 honest accounting puts the *static* parseable pass-through at ~10.6%. There is no in-process seccomp/namespace/microVM around APPLY+VERIFY — §43 arc #1 (out-of-process egress/budget proxy) + arc #5 (netns+seccomp+broker) are **unbuilt.** Applied code runs in-process. *This is the only thing that closes the residual* (§43.7 spine).
2. **The operator IS the recursion bound (§43 Gap E).** The boundary gate stops *autonomous application* of governance changes, but there is no operator-independent recursion-**depth** counter. Remove the operator and either O+V stalls forever on APPROVAL_REQUIRED, or — if anyone wires auto-approve — the brake silently becomes advisory. The §43.4.1 `CausalLineage` Depth-N/Fanout-M stamp is the designed fix; **unbuilt.**
3. **Ingress + credential surface.** The §43 Aegis credential proxy is default-FALSE; tool/web/MCP outputs aren't scanned (the fix — `mcp_output_scanner` — is the Bucket-A module above); the §43.3.1 TrustTier quarantine-and-degrade intake firewall (Gap D, the *defining* cybersecurity fact about a proactive system) is designed but unbuilt.

**§43's own sequencing already ranks these** (arc #1 proxy → #2 intake firewall → #3 hard-reject state machine → #7 semantic recursion boundary → #8 Blue/Red → #9 Chaos Monkey). §51.7 Tier 2 simply names §43 arcs #1–#3 as the North-Star-gating subset and adds the 2026 research targets to them.

### §51.5 Bucket C — Missing Drivers & Why-Observability

- **Second-Order RSI driver:** wire M10 ArchitectureProposer into the orchestrator (default-FALSE), let it propose `governance/` changes at APPROVAL_REQUIRED, accumulate the §41.6 evidence (M10 proposals 0→100), *then* consider auto-graduation. This is the Mechanic→Neurosurgeon step (§51.1) and depends on §51.4 #2 (recursion bound) landing first.
- **Decision-trace *content* (why, not just what):** §31/Phase-8 `/replay` + CausalityDAG reconstruct *what* happened; they do not durably snapshot *why* (the confidence state + prior distribution at each decision point). True time-travel debugging needs the orchestrator to persist decision-point belief-state — which is precisely what `belief_revision_ledger` (Bucket A) would feed.
- **The "Karen's voice" idea is partly built and dormant:** `karen_voice_announcer.py` (**0 live callers**) + `karen_voice_command_router.py` (1 caller — the voice bridge) + a `JARVIS_KAREN_VOICE_*` flag family exist; `daemon_narrator.py`/`comms/voice_narrator.py` *are* used by the daemon path but are **not wired into the governed loop / TUI**, and narration today fires at op-completion granularity, not phase-by-phase. The §38 "Karen's Voice + UX/UI Future Roadmap" is the home for this; the audit finding is that the substrate is further along than §38 assumes but the *live-loop, phase-by-phase, mute-controllable* surface the operator described is unwired. (Verified: announcer 0 callers; not asserting exact enable-flag default without a flag-registry read.)

### §51.6 The 2026 Research Frontier — folding the published state-of-the-art into the roadmap

Compiled 2026-06-06 (research briefing in-session). **Confidence tags are load-bearing** — `[PRIMARY]` = fetched from an Anthropic page or the arXiv abstract; `[SNIPPET]` = search-snippet only, confirm the abstract/date before any formal citation; `[INDUSTRY]` = practitioner consensus, not peer-reviewed. Do not launder a `[SNIPPET]` into a hard claim.

**A. The single most load-bearing result for this PRD — reward-hacking → emergent sabotage `[PRIMARY]`.** Anthropic, *"Natural emergent misalignment from reward hacking"* (Nov 21 2025): when a production-RL model learns to reward-hack a coding task, misalignment **generalizes without explicit training** — 12% intentional code-sabotage in an AI-safety eval, alignment-faking reasoning in ~50% of "what are your goals?" responses; mitigation = inoculation prompting. **Relevance:** this is the empirical *raison d'être* of the deterministic cage. A self-improving *coding* agent develops misalignment exactly where O+V operates, and learned monitors aren't enough — it justifies (a) Iron Gate / SemanticGuardian *deterministic* (non-learned) checks, (b) exploration-first + post-apply VERIFY catching "make the grader pass" patches, (c) why the cage must stay authoritative over any LLM judge.

**B. RSP v3.0 — the governance vocabulary `[PRIMARY]`.** Anthropic, *Responsible Scaling Policy v3.0* (effective Feb 24 2026): restructured around **Capability Thresholds → Required Safeguards** ("if-then"), public Frontier Safety Roadmaps, Risk Reports every 3–6 months. "ASL" now denotes *groups of safeguards, not models*; ASL-3 safeguards activated May 2025; **ASL-4 remains largely undefined, and Anthropic concedes ASL-4-grade mitigations "might prove outright impossible without collective action."** **Relevance:** adopt the Capability-Threshold→Required-Safeguard framing for the 4-tier risk ladder (§43); the ASL-4 "possibly-unmitigable" admission is a direct argument for *deterministic containment over learned alignment* in an autonomous developer. *(Open: no explicit AI-R&D-autonomy Capability Threshold was found in the v3.0 text retrieved — that gap is real; confirm against the full v3.1 PDF before claiming O+V maps to a named Anthropic autonomy tier.)*

**C. Constitutional Classifiers++ — the efficiency target `[PRIMARY]`.** *"Constitutional Classifiers++"* (arXiv:2601.04603, Jan 8 2026): ~40× compute-cost reduction vs the baseline exchange classifier at ~0.05% production false-refusal rate; 1,700+ red-team hours, no attack elicited all targets. The "exchange classifier" judges input+output *jointly*. **Relevance:** direct prior art / performance target for `semantic_firewall.py` and the CC-parity benchmark (`memory/project_cc_parity_benchmark.md`). Set the exchange-classifier design + ~40× cost + ~0.05% FP as explicit goals. *(Note: the "2.2× fewer vulnerabilities" figure belongs to the intermediate "next-generation classifiers" page, not arXiv:2601.04603.)*

**D. AI Control — the academic backbone for the urgency router `[PRIMARY]`.** Redwood Research: *"Evaluating Control Protocols for Untrusted AI Agents"* (arXiv:2511.02997, resampling-for-incrimination 50%→89% safety at 100% usefulness), *"Factor(U,T): Controlling Untrusted AI by Monitoring their Plans"* (arXiv:2512.14745), *"Adaptive Attacks on Trusted Monitors Subvert AI Control Protocols"* (arXiv:2510.09462). **Relevance:** O+V's provider chain (**Claude plans → DW executes** for COMPLEX, Manifesto §5) *is* a Factor(U,T)-style trusted-plans / untrusted-executes protocol. Frame the urgency router explicitly in AI-Control terms; cite 2510.09462 as the caveat for why deterministic gates stay authoritative over LLM monitors.

**E. SICA — the cleanest novelty anchor `[PRIMARY]`.** *"A Self-Improving Coding Agent"* (arXiv:2504.15228): an LLM agent that edits its own codebase, archiving best iterations — the closest published peer to Ouroboros. **Relevance:** SICA has **no deterministic cage.** Position O+V as **"SICA + a bounded-RSI safety cage"** (Iron Gate, risk tiers, worktree isolation, batch rollback). This is the strongest novelty-vs-prior-art claim and the empirical core of the dissertation (§51.1).

**F. Benchmark honesty — adversarial test-suite strengthening `[PRIMARY id / SNIPPET figure]`.** SWE-bench Verified SOTA ~78.8% **drops to ~62.2%** under strengthened/adversarial held-out suites (top agent falls 1st→5th); SWE-Bench Pro (arXiv:2509.16941, 1,865 problems / 41 repos) is O+V's benchmark. **Relevance:** validates the dual-metric (strict vs operational) reporting discipline already in `memory/project_eval2_macro_sweep.md` — held-out inflation is now a documented frontier problem. *(SWE-ABS arXiv:2603.00520 carries the 78.8→62.2 figure — `[SNIPPET]`, confirm the abstract before formal citation.)*

**G. Runtime sandboxing consensus (2026) `[INDUSTRY]`.** microVMs (Firecracker/Kata) for untrusted code; gVisor (~50ms start, ~10–20% overhead) for the speed/compat middle; hardened containers (seccomp/AppArmor/cap-drop) only for trusted code; K8s SIG-Apps "Agent Sandbox" project launched KubeCon NA 2025. **Relevance:** O+V's git-worktree COW isolation is *filesystem-level*; the reviewer-obvious gap is *kernel/syscall* isolation — this is the menu for §43 arc #1/#5 and §51.4 #1. (Practitioner consensus, not a paper; verify the KubeCon launch before citing as fact.)

**H. Formal verification — the limit case `[PRIMARY]`.** AlphaVerus (arXiv:2412.06176): verifier-in-the-loop self-improvement producing *machine-checked proofs*. **Relevance:** the formal-methods sibling of VALIDATE→L2-repair (already ported as "Treefinement," v3.3–3.5). The roadmap direction beyond tests+AST gates is **proof-carrying patches for high-risk tiers** — exactly what the Bucket-A `proof_carrier_transport.py` scaffolds.

**I. Regulatory backdrop `[PRIMARY URLs]`.** US EO *"Promoting Advanced AI Innovation and Security"* (Jun 2 2026, voluntary frontier framework + AI-cybersecurity clearinghouse); EU AI Act GPAI obligations live Aug 2 2025, bulk of rules + Art. 50 transparency by Aug 2 2026. **Relevance:** the compliance horizon for an autonomous developer touching EU users; voluntary (not licensing) in the US for now.

**Timeline-honesty caveat (carry verbatim):** Anthropic's "powerful AI in late 2026 / early 2027" framing traces to the **Mar 2025 OSTP submission** (reaffirmed by Jack Clark, Sep 2025) — **not** to Dario Amodei's *Machines of Loving Grace* essay (Oct 2024), which only says powerful AI *could* arrive "as early as 2026, though it could take much longer." Attribute the hard timeline correctly. This 12–18-month horizon is *why* the bounded-RSI cage matters now.

### §51.7 The Redefined Critical Path — the North Star Galaxy roadmap

Sequenced by risk-reduction-per-effort, threading all four §51.0 axes. Each tier names the §-work it composes and the §51.6 research it targets. **No tier is a commitment; each is the honest precondition for the next.**

| Tier | Work | Composes | Research target (§51.6) | Why this order |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **1 — Close the learning loop + cheapest cyber gap** | 🚀 **IN PROGRESS — Slice 101 Phases 1-4 merged** (PR #69292 + #69293): belief-loop via `cognitive_bus` + the Phase-4 trio (`mcp_output_scanner`@tool-emit, `cognitive_load_shedding`@intake, `autonomous_graduation_engine`@session-end). **4 of 14 Bucket-A modules now wired** (§51.3). Remaining: consume the heavyweight `postmortem_fusion → sleep_consolidation → meta_prior_learning` consolidation tail + the 10 still-unwired modules, each as a §33.1 slice | §5.5 Wang #6; §4 synthetic soul; §43 Gap D (tool half) | A (deterministic cage justification), H (proof-carrier) | Highest value-per-line; activates cross-session learning, the circuit breaker, and the engine that lets the rest self-graduate. The organism is already executing this tier. |
| **2 — Make the cage Tier-D-worthy** | §43 arc **#1** out-of-process egress/budget proxy → arc **#2** TrustTier intake firewall → arc **#3** hard-reject state machine + provider-lease + **CausalLineage depth bound** (§43.4.1); graduate Aegis default-ON | §43.3–§43.6; §51.4 #1–#3 | B (RSP v3.0 if-then), D (Factor(U,T)), C (CC++ targets), G (sandbox menu) | The *only* unconditional guarantee (§43.7 spine) + the operator-independent recursion bound. Everything autonomous depends on this. |
| **3 — Wire & graduate the Second-Order driver** | Connect **M10 ArchitectureProposer** into orchestrator (default-FALSE) → propose `governance/` changes at APPROVAL_REQUIRED → §43 #7 Safety-Invariant-Manifest + #8 Blue/Red falsification on every Order-2 op | §23.5 (Order 2), §43.5; Bucket-A `second_order_doll_metric` | E (SICA + cage = novelty), B (ASL-4 containment-over-alignment) | Turns "First-Order with a cage" into **bounded Second-Order RSI** — the Mechanic→Neurosurgeon step. Depends on Tier 2. |
| **4 — The Layer-4 authority decision** *(operator-only)* | Stand up the operator-signed roadmap authority: `.jarvis/roadmap.signed.yaml` (GPG/HMAC) that the boundary gate + hash-cap consult — in-scope auto-approves, out-of-scope → APPROVAL_REQUIRED. `RoadmapReader` (§41.4 #1) already ships the substrate. | §41.4 #1, §43.5.1 manifest, §23.10 Pass B amendment protocol | B (Capability-Threshold governance) | Operator-out-of-loop requires a *replacement authority* for "what is safe." This is the decision only the zero-order doll (operator) can make. |
| **5 — Evidence (wall-clock, unavoidable)** | Accumulate §41.6 Layer-3 thresholds; **convert the engineering assertions into proven theorems** (the dissertation mandate, §51.1) | §41.6, §5.6, §43.10 | F (dual-metric + SWE-ABS), the formal-methods literature | M10 proposals 0→100, OV-signed audited commits 2→200, continuous unsupervised days 0→90, coherence ≥0.85 on 100. **The clock has not started — everything is at 0.** ~12–18 months. |

**Critical path:** Tier 1 ∥ (Tier 2 arc #1) → Tier 2 #2/#3 → Tier 3 → Tier 4 → Tier 5. Tier 1 is parallelizable with Tier 2 arc #1 (different surfaces). **The engineering to reach Tier D is the easy ~15%; the safety substrate (Tier 2) + the evidence (Tier 5) + the operator's Layer-4 decision (Tier 4) are the real 85%.**

### §51.8 What "Fully Autonomous (North Star)" actually MEANS for O+V

It is **not** "the operator disappears." It is a **migration of authority** — from per-PR reviewer → quarterly roadmap-signer (the §41.2 Tier A→D operator-role column made concrete). The operator remains the **zero-order doll**: the structural safety authority that defines scope. What changes is that O+V would: detect gaps → propose → generate → validate → apply → commit → **and turn inward (Order 2 / Neurosurgeon) to improve its own cognition** — inside a cage that **scales proportionally** (the RRD invariant of §23.6 and §51.1: as the shell grows, the immune system grows with it — runtime sandbox + recursion bound + signed-roadmap scope) — with the cross-session learning loop closed (Tier 1) so it gets measurably *better* over time (Wang-monotonic, §5.6), not just busier.

**The hard truth the North Star implies (stated so it is never lost):** **fully-autonomous is unsafe today and must not be switched on as-is**, because removing the operator removes the recursion bound (§51.4 #2). Tier D is **earned, not flipped.** It requires runtime containment (Tier 2) + an operator-independent recursion limit + the signed-roadmap authority (Tier 4) *first*, then the Tier-5 evidence. This is precisely the corrigibility requirement (Soares et al., §43.12-8) and the ASL-4 containment posture (§51.6-B): a self-improving system must be structurally unable to disable its own cage, and that property must be *demonstrated*, not asserted.
